134:     { id: 'kimi-k2.5', name: 'Kimi K2.5' },
135:     { id: 'MiniMax-M2.5', name: 'MiniMax M2.5' },
136: ]
137: 
138: const selectedModelId = ref<string>(modelList[0].id)
139: const modelName = computed(() => {
140:     const found = modelList.find(item => item.id === selectedModelId.value)
141:     return found?.name || selectedModelId.value
142: })
143: 
144: const messages = ref<Message[]>([])
145: const userInput = ref('')
146: const isLoading = ref(false)
147: const enableThinking = ref(false)
148: 
149: const scrollToBottom = async () => {
150:     await nextTick()
151:     const messagesArea = document.querySelector('.messages-area')
152:     if (messagesArea) {
153:         messagesArea.scrollTop = messagesArea.scrollHeight
154:     }
155: }
156: 
157: const formatTime = (date: Date) => {
158:     return date.toLocaleTimeString('zh-CN', {
159:         hour: '2-digit',
160:         minute: '2-digit'
161:     })
162: }
163: 
164: // 处理 <think>...</think> 标签，将推理内容显示为小字
165: const processThinkContent = (content: string): string => {
166:     const thinkMatch = content.match(/<think>([\s\S]*?)<\/think>/)
167:     if (thinkMatch) {
168:         const thinkContent = thinkMatch[1]
169:         const smallThinkContent = `<small style="font-size: 0.8em; color: #6b7280;">${thinkContent}</small>`
170:         return content.replace(thinkMatch[0], smallThinkContent)
171:     }
172:     return content
173: }
174: 
175: const processedContent = (content: string): string => {
176:     return processThinkContent(content)
177: }
178: 
179: // 处理推理内容（reasoning_content）
180: const processReasoningContent = (content: string): string => {
181:     return `<small style="font-size: 0.8em; color: #6b7280;">${content}</small>`
182: }
183: 
184: const clearMessages = () => {
185:     messages.value = []
186:     messages.value.push({
187:         role: 'assistant',
188:         content: '你好！我是湛明 AI 助手，有什么可以帮助你的吗？',
189:         timestamp: new Date()
190:     })
191:     ElMessage.success('已开始新对话')
192: }
193: 
194: const sendMessage = async () => {
195:     if (!userInput.value.trim() || isLoading.value) {
196:         return
197:     }
198: 
199:     const userMessage: Message = {
200:         role: 'user',
201:         content: userInput.value.trim(),
202:         timestamp: new Date()
203:     }
204: 
205:     messages.value.push(userMessage)
206:     userInput.value = ''
207:     isLoading.value = true
208: 
209:     await scrollToBottom()
210: 
211:     try {
212:         // 调用后端 API（流式模式）
213:         const response = await fetch('/api/app/chat/completions', {
214:             method: 'POST',
215:             headers: {
216:                 'Content-Type': 'application/json',
217:                 'Accept': 'text/event-stream',
218:             },
219: body: JSON.stringify({
220:                 model: selectedModelId.value,
221:                 messages: messages.value.map(m => ({
222:                     role: m.role,
223:                     content: m.content
224:                 })),
225:                 stream: true,
226:                 thinking: enableThinking.value
227:             })
228:         })
229: 
230:         if (!response.ok) {
231:             const errorData = await response.json().catch(() => ({}))
232:             throw new Error(`API 请求失败：${response.status} - ${errorData.message || response.statusText}`)
233:         }
234: 
235:         // 添加空的 AI 消息容器
236:         const aiMessageIndex = messages.value.length
237:         messages.value.push({
238:             role: 'assistant',
239:             content: '',
240:             timestamp: new Date()
241:         })
242: 
243:         // 处理流式响应
244:         const reader = response.body?.getReader()
245:         if (!reader) {
246:             throw new Error('无法读取响应流')
247:         }
248: 
249:         const decoder = new TextDecoder('utf-8')
250:         let buffer = ''
251: 
252:         while (true) {
253:             const { done, value } = await reader.read()
254:             if (done) break
255: 
256:             buffer += decoder.decode(value, { stream: true })
257:             const lines = buffer.split('\n')
258:             buffer = lines.pop() || ''
259: 
260:             for (const line of lines) {
261:                 const trimmedLine = line.trim()
262:                 if (!trimmedLine || !trimmedLine.startsWith('data:')) continue
263:                 if (trimmedLine === 'data: [DONE]') continue
264: 
265:                 try {
266:                     const json = JSON.parse(trimmedLine.slice(6))
267:                     const delta = json.choices?.[0]?.delta
268: 
269:                     if (delta?.content) {
270:                         messages.value[aiMessageIndex].content += delta.content
271:                         await scrollToBottom()
272:                     }
273:                 }
274:                 catch (e) {
275:                     console.warn('解析 SSE 数据失败:', e)
276:                 }
277:             }
278:         }
279:     }
280:     catch (error) {
281:         console.error('Error sending message:', error)
282:         const errorMessage: Message = {
283:             role: 'assistant',
284:             content: `抱歉，发生了一个错误：${error instanceof Error ? error.message : '未知错误'}`,
285:             timestamp: new Date()
286:         }
287:         messages.value.push(errorMessage)
288:         ElMessage.error('发送消息失败')
289:     }
290:     finally {
291:         isLoading.value = false
292:         await scrollToBottom()
293:     }
294: }
295: 
296: const handleModelChange = (command: string) => {
297:     selectedModelId.value = command
298:     ElMessage.success(`已切换到 ${modelName.value}`)
299: }
300:

27:      * @returns 没有显式返回值，但会更新 state 中的 lists 状态。
28:      */
29:     const getArticleList = async (config: ApiConfig, $api: ApiType = api) => {
30:         // 如果当前已有数据且请求的路径和页码相同，则无需重复请求
31:         if (state.lists.data.length > 0 && config.path === state.lists.path && config.page === 1) {
32:             return
33:         }
34: 
35:         // 发起 GET 请求获取文章列表数据
36:         const { code, data } = await $api.get<ResDataLists<Article>>('frontend/article/list', { ...config, path: undefined, cache: true })
37: 
38:         // 请求成功且返回数据时，处理返回的数据
39:         if (code === 200 && data) {
40:             // 解构并赋值返回的数据，同时修正部分字段的值
41:             const {

44:                 hasNext = 0,
45:                 hasPrev = 0,
46:                 page,

50:                 page: config.page, // 修正页码信息
51:             }
52: 
53:             // 更新 state 中的 lists 状态
54:             state.lists = {
55:                 data: page === 1 ? list : state.lists.data.concat(list), // 根据页码合并文章列表数据
56:                 hasNext, // 是否有下一页
57:                 hasPrev, // 是否有上一页
58:                 page: (page || 1) + 1, // 更新当前页码

114:

119:         if (state.item.data && state.item.data._id === id) {
120:             if (status) {
121:                 state.item.data.like++
122:             }
123:             else {
124:                 state.item.data.like--
125:             }
126:             state.item.data.like_status = status
127:         }
128:

130:         const index = state.lists.data.findIndex((item: Article) => item._id === id)

134:             if (status) {
135:                 obj.like++
136:             }
137:             else {
138:                 obj.like--
139:             }
140:             obj.like_status = status
141:             state.lists.data.splice(index, 1, obj)
142:         }
143:     }
144:

<content>1: import { toValue, onUnmounted } from 'vue'
2: import type { Ref } from 'vue'

10:     stream: false,
11:     temperature: 0.8,
12:     top_p: 1,
13:     top_k: 5,
14:     max_tokens: 16384,
15:     presence_penalty: 0,
16:     frequency_penalty: 0,
17:     seed: 1,
18:     stop: [],
19:     stream_options: { include_usage: false },
20: }
21: 
22: export function useMakeAutosuggestion(modelOptions: Ref<ModelAiptions>, scrollFn?: () => void) {
23:     const chatStore = useChatStore()
24: 
25:     let abortController: AbortController | null = null
26: 
27:     onUnmounted(() => {
28:         if (abortController) {
29:             abortController.abort()
30:             abortController = null
31:         }
32:     })
33: 
34:     const makeRequestData = (model: string, message: Message): CompletionRequest | null => {
35:         if (!model) {
36:             return null
37:         }
38: 
39:         chatStore.addMessage(message)
40:         const messages = chatStore.messages
41: 
42:         for (let i = 1; i < messages.length; i++) {
43:             const current = messages[i]
44:             const next = messages[i + 1]
45:             if (current.role === 'user' && next && next.role !== 'assistant') {
46:                 messages.splice(i + 1, 0, { role: 'assistant', content: '' })
47:             }
48:             if (current.role === 'assistant' && next && next.role !== 'user') {
49:                 messages.splice(i + 1, 0, { role: 'user', content: '' })
50:             }
51:         }
52: 
53:         if (messages.length > 0 && messages[messages.length - 1].role !== 'user') {
54:             messages.push({ role: 'user', content: '' })
55:         }
56: 
57:         const lastUserMessage = messages[messages.length - 1].content
58:         const historyMessages = messages
59:             .slice(0, -1)
60:             .filter((msg): msg is Message => msg.role !== 'system')
61:             .map(msg => ({
62:                 role: msg.role,
63:                 content: msg.content,
64:             }))
65: 
66:         scrollFn && scrollFn()
67: 
68:         return {
69:             ...defaultModelOptions,
70:             ...toValue(modelOptions),
71:             model,
72:             messages: [
73:                 ...historyMessages,
74:                 { role: 'user' as const, content: lastUserMessage },
75:             ],
76:         }
77:     }
78: 
79:     const handleStreamResponse = async (response: Response) => {
80:         const reader = response.body?.getReader()
81:         if (!reader) {
82:             console.error('Reader is not available.')
83:             return
84:         }
85: 
86:         const decoder = new TextDecoder('utf-8')
87: 
88:         chatStore.addMessage({ role: 'assistant', content: '' })
89: 
90:         let buffer = ''
91: 
92:         try {
93:             while (true) {
94:                 const { done, value } = await reader.read()
95: 
96:                 if (done) {
97:                     console.log('Stream completed')
98:                     if (buffer.trim()) {
99:                         processSSELine(buffer.trim())
100:                     }
101:                     return
102:                 }
103: 
104:                 buffer += decoder.decode(value, { stream: true })
105: 
106:                 const events = buffer.split('\n\n')
107:                 buffer = events.pop() || ''
108: 
109:                 for (const event of events) {
110:                     if (!event.trim()) continue
111: 
112:                     const lines = event.split('\n')
113:                     for (const line of lines) {
114:                         await processSSELine(line.trim())
115:                     }
116:                 }
117:             }
118:         }
119:         catch (error) {
120:             console.error('Error reading stream:', error)
121:             throw error
122:         }
123:     }
124: 
125:     const processSSELine = async (line: string) => {
126:         if (!line) return
127: 
128:         if (line.startsWith('data: ')) {
129:             const data = line.slice(6).trim()
130: 
131:             if (data === '[DONE]') {
132:                 console.log('Stream done signal received')
133:                 return
134:             }
135: 
136:             if (data) {
137:                 try {
138:                     const json = JSON.parse(data)
139: 
140:                     if (json.error) {
141:                         throw new Error(json.error)
142:                     }
143: 
144:                     if (json.choices && json.choices[0]?.delta) {
145:                         const delta = json.choices[0].delta
146: 
147:                         if ('content' in delta && delta.content !== null && delta.content !== undefined) {
148:                             chatStore.messages[chatStore.messages.length - 1].content += delta.content
149:                             scrollFn && scrollFn()
150:                         }
151: 
152:                         if ('reasoning_content' in delta && delta.reasoning_content !== null && delta.reasoning_content !== undefined) {
153:                             const sanitizedContent = DOMPurify.sanitize(delta.reasoning_content)
154:                             const thinkContent = `<small style="font-size: 0.8em; color: blue;">${sanitizedContent}</small>`
155:                             chatStore.messages[chatStore.messages.length - 1].content += thinkContent
156:                             scrollFn && scrollFn()
157:                         }
158:                     }
159:                 }
160:                 catch (e) {
161:                     if (e instanceof SyntaxError) {
162:                         console.warn('Failed to parse SSE data:', data.substring(0, 100))
163:                     }
164:                     else {
165:                         throw e
166:                     }
167:                 }
168:             }
169:         }
170:     }
171: 
172:     const makeAutosuggestion = async (model: string, message: Message): Promise<string | void> => {
173:         const requestData = makeRequestData(model, message)
174:         if (!requestData) {
175:             ElMessage.error('未选择模型')
176:             return
177:         }
178: 
179:         const isStream = toValue(modelOptions).stream === true
180: 
181:         if (abortController) {
182:             abortController.abort()
183:         }
184:         abortController = new AbortController()
185: 
186:         try {
187:             if (isStream) {
188:                 console.log('Sending stream request to:', config.api + 'app/chat/completions')
189: 
190:                 const response = await fetch(config.api + 'app/chat/completions', {
191:                     method: 'POST',
192:                     headers: {
193:                         'Content-Type': 'application/json',
194:                         'Accept': 'text/event-stream',
195:                     },
196:                     body: JSON.stringify(requestData),
197:                     signal: abortController.signal,
198:                 })
199: 
200:                 console.log('Response status:', response.status, response.statusText)
201: 
202:                 if (!response.ok) {
203:                     const errorText = await response.text()
204:                     let errorMsg = `HTTP ${response.status}`
205:                     try {
206:                         const errorData = JSON.parse(errorText)
207:                         errorMsg = errorData.message || errorMsg
208:                     }
209:                     catch {
210:                         errorMsg = errorText || errorMsg
211:                     }
212:                     throw new Error(errorMsg)
213:                 }
214: 
215:                 await handleStreamResponse(response)
216:             }
217:             else {
218:                 const response = await api.post('app/chat/completions', requestData)
219:                 if (response.code !== 200) {
220:                     throw new Error(response.message || '请求失败')
221:                 }
222:                 return response.data
223:             }
224:         }
225:         catch (error) {
226:             if (error instanceof Error && error.name === 'AbortError') {
227:                 console.log('Request aborted')
228:                 return
229:             }
230:             console.error('Error during chatCompletion:', error)
231:             ElMessage.error(error instanceof Error ? error.message : '生成建议失败')
232:             throw error
233:         }
234:         finally {
235:             abortController = null
236:         }
237:     }
238: 
239:     return {
240:         makeAutosuggestion,
241:     }
242: }

<content>1: <template>
2:   <div class="markdown-renderer">
3:     <component :is="renderedContent" />
4:   </div>

7: <script setup lang="ts">

9: 
10: interface Props {
11:   content: string
12: }
13: 
14: const props = defineProps<Props>()
15: 
16: const renderedContent = computed(() => {
17:   const html = parseMarkdown(props.content)
18:   return {
19:     template: `<div class="markdown-body">${html}</div>`,
20:   }
21: })
22: 
23: function parseMarkdown(markdown: string): string {
24:   let html = markdown
25: 
26:   html = html.replace(/^### (.*$)/gim, '<h3>$1</h3>')
27:   html = html.replace(/^## (.*$)/gim, '<h2>$1</h2>')
28:   html = html.replace(/^# (.*$)/gim, '<h1>$1</h1>')
29: 
30:   html = html.replace(/\*\*(.*?)\*\*/gim, '<strong>$1</strong>')
31:   html = html.replace(/\*(.*?)\*/gim, '<em>$1</em>')
32: 
33:   html = html.replace(/!\[(.*?)\]\((.*?)\)/gim, '<img src="$2" alt="$1" loading="lazy" />')
34: 
35:   html = html.replace(/\[(.*?)\]\((.*?)\)/gim, '<a href="$2" target="_blank" rel="noopener">$1</a>')
36: 
37:   html = html.replace(/`{3}(\w+)?\n([\s\S]*?)`{3}/gim, '<pre><code class="language-$1">$2</code></pre>')
38:   html = html.replace(/`([^`]+)`/gim, '<code>$1</code>')
39: 
40:   html = html.replace(/^> (.*$)/gim, '<blockquote>$1</blockquote>')
41: 
42:   html = html.replace(/^\* (.*$)/gim, '<li>$1</li>')
43:   html = html.replace(/(<li>.*<\/li>)/s, '<ul>$1</ul>')
44: 
45:   html = html.replace(/^(\d+)\. (.*$)/gim, '<li>$2</li>')
46: 
47:   html = html.replace(/\n\n/gim, '</p><p>')
48:   html = html.replace(/\n/gim, '<br />')
49: 
50:   html = `<p>${html}</p>`
51: 
52:   html = html.replace(/<p><\/p>/gim, '')
53:   html = html.replace(/<p>(<[hulbo])/gim, '$1')
54:   html = html.replace(/(<\/[hulbo][^>]*>)<\/p>/gim, '$1')
55: 
56:   return html
57: }
58: </script>
59: 
60: <style scoped>
61: .markdown-renderer {
62:   width: 100%;
63: }
64:

66:   font-family: Inter, -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, 'Segoe UI', sans-serif;
67:   font-size: 16px;
68:   line-height: 1.8;
69:   color: var(--color-text-primary);
70:   word-wrap: break-word;

<content>1: import { ref, computed, watchEffect } from 'vue'
2: 
3: export type ThemeMode = 'light' | 'dark' | 'auto'
4: 
5: const THEME_STORAGE_KEY = 'theme-mode'
6: 
7: export const useTheme = () => {
8:   const theme = ref<ThemeMode>(
9:     (localStorage.getItem(THEME_STORAGE_KEY) as ThemeMode) || 'auto'
10:   )
11: 
12:   const actualTheme = computed(() => {
13:     if (theme.value === 'auto') {
14:       return window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)').matches
15:         ? 'dark'
16:         : 'light'
17:     }
18:     return theme.value
19:   })
20: 
21:   const isDark = computed(() => actualTheme.value === 'dark')
22: 
23:   const setTheme = (newTheme: ThemeMode) => {
24:     theme.value = newTheme
25:     localStorage.setItem(THEME_STORAGE_KEY, newTheme)
26:   }
27: 
28:   const toggleTheme = () => {
29:     const nextTheme: ThemeMode = actualTheme.value === 'dark' ? 'light' : 'dark'
30:     setTheme(nextTheme)
31:   }
32: 
33:   watchEffect(() => {
34:     document.documentElement.setAttribute('data-theme', actualTheme.value)
35: 
36:     const metaThemeColor = document.querySelector('meta[name="theme-color"]')
37:     if (metaThemeColor) {
38:       metaThemeColor.setAttribute(
39:         'content',
40:         actualTheme.value === 'dark' ? '#000000' : '#FFFFFF'
41:       )
42:     }
43:   })
44: 
45:   const mediaQuery = window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)')
46:   const handleMediaChange = () => {
47:     if (theme.value === 'auto') {
48:       document.documentElement.setAttribute(
49:         'data-theme',
50:         mediaQuery.matches ? 'dark' : 'light'
51:       )
52:     }
53:   }
54: 
55:   mediaQuery.addEventListener('change', handleMediaChange)
56: 
57:   return {
58:     theme,
59:     actualTheme,
60:     isDark,
61:     setTheme,
62:     toggleTheme,

122: // 初始化网格

124:     cellsX = Math.floor(innerWidth / 16)
125:     cellsY = Math.floor(innerHeight / 16)
126:     
127:     const newGrid: Array<Array<boolean>> = []
128:     for (let i = 0; i < cellsY; i++) {
129:         const row = new Array(cellsX).fill(CellState.DEAD)
130:         for (let j = 0; j < cellsX; j++) {
131:             if (Math.random() < 0.2) {
132:                 row[j] = !CellState.DEAD
133:             }
134:         }
135:         newGrid.push(row)
136:     }
137:     grid.value = newGrid
138: }
139: 
140: const nullCheck = (y: number | null, x: number | null): boolean | null => {
141:     return y !== null && x !== null ? grid.value[y][x].valueOf() : null
142: }
143: 
144: const neighbours = (outerKey: number, innerKey: number): number => {
145:     const leftX = innerKey - 1 < 0 ? null : innerKey - 1
146:     const rightX = innerKey + 1 >= grid.value[outerKey].length ? null : innerKey + 1
147:     const centerX = innerKey
148:     const centerY = outerKey
149:     const topY = outerKey - 1 < 0 ? null : outerKey - 1
150:     const bottomY = outerKey + 1 >= grid.value.length ? null : outerKey + 1
151: 
152:     return [
153:         nullCheck(topY, leftX),
154:         nullCheck(topY, centerX),
155:         nullCheck(topY, rightX),
156:         nullCheck(centerY, leftX),
157:         nullCheck(centerY, rightX),
158:         nullCheck(bottomY, leftX),
159:         nullCheck(bottomY, centerX),
160:         nullCheck(bottomY, rightX),
161:     ].filter(x => x).length
162: }
163: 
164: const userInput = (ok: number, ik: number): void => {
165:     if (inputEnabled.value) {
166:         grid.value = grid.value.map((row, a_ok) => {
167:             return a_ok === ok ? row.map((cell, a_ik) => {
168:                 return a_ik === ik ? !cell : cell
169:             }) : row
170:         })
171:     }
172: }
173: 
174: const step = (): void => {
175:     generation.value++
176:     grid.value = grid.value.map((row, ok) => {
177:         return row.map((cell, ik) => {
178:             if (neighbours(ok, ik) === 3) {
179:                 return CellState.ALIVE
180:             }
181:             if (neighbours(ok, ik) <= 1) {
182:                 return CellState.DEAD
183:             }
184:             if (neighbours(ok, ik) >= 4) {
185:                 return CellState.DEAD
186:             }
187:             return cell
188:         })
189:     })
190: }
191: 
192: const togglePlay = (): void => {
193:     if (playEnabled.value) {
194:         clearInterval(intervalId.value)
195:     }
196:     else {
197:         intervalId.value = setInterval(step, SPEED)
198:     }
199:     playEnabled.value = !playEnabled.value
200: }
201: 
202: const toggleIcon = (): void => {
203:     controlsHidden.value = window.pageYOffset > 150
204: }
205: 
206: onMounted(() => {
207:     initGrid()
208:     window.addEventListener('scroll', toggleIcon)
209: })
210: 
211: onUnmounted(() => {
212:     window.removeEventListener('scroll', toggleIcon)
213:     if (intervalId.value) {
214:         clearInterval(intervalId.value)
215:     }
216: })
217: 
218: const headTitle = ref('Game of Life - 湛明')
219: useHead({
220:     title: headTitle,
221:     meta: [
222:         {
223:             name: 'description',
224:             content: 'John Horton Conway\'s Game of Life',
225:         },
226:     ],
227: })
228: </script>

# 前端代码检查报告

## 一、安全问题 🔴

### 1. XSS漏洞（严重）

| 文件位置 | 问题描述 | 严重程度 |
|---------|---------|---------|
| `frontend-article.vue:35` | `v-html="addTarget(articleData.html)"` - 直接渲染服务器返回的HTML，未进行消毒处理 | **高** |
| `frontend-ai.vue:33` | `v-html="processedContent(message.content)"` - AI返回内容直接渲染，可能包含恶意脚本 | **高** |
| `frontend-about.vue:28` | `v-html="aboutHtml"` - 虽然当前为空字符串，但存在潜在XSS风险 | **中** |
| `MarkdownRenderer.vue:16-21` | 使用动态模板渲染HTML，`template` 直接拼接未经验证的HTML | **高** |

**建议**：使用 `DOMPurify.sanitize()` 处理所有动态HTML（已安装但未在关键位置使用）。

---

### 2. 敏感信息存储（中等）

| 文件位置 | 问题描述 | 严重程度 |
|---------|---------|---------|
| `router.ts:48,58` | Cookie存储认证token（`user`, `b_user`），未设置 `HttpOnly`、`Secure`、`SameSite` 属性 | **高** |
| `app.vue:34-36` | 用户信息存储在全局store和cookie中，包含用户名、邮箱等敏感信息 | **中** |
| `useTheme.ts:9,25` | localStorage存储主题设置（低风险） | **低** |

---

### 3. API安全问题

| 文件位置 | 问题描述 | 严重程度 |
|---------|---------|---------|
| `upload-api.ts:1` | 硬编码外部上传API地址 `https://php.mmxiaowu.com` | **中** |
| `index-client.ts:7-14` | 请求拦截器未添加认证token | **中** |
| `frontend-ai.vue:213-228` | AI API调用未验证响应来源，可能被劫持 | **中** |

---

### 4. 用户输入验证不足

| 文件位置 | 问题描述 | 严重程度 |
|---------|---------|---------|
| `sign-in.vue:54-55` | 仅检查字段是否为空，未验证长度和格式 | **中** |
| `sign-up.vue:63-79` | 前端验证可被绕过，需后端二次验证 | **中** |
| `frontend-comment.vue:89-91` | 评论内容仅检查是否为空，无长度限制和内容过滤 | **中** |

---

## 二、代码质量问题 🟡

### 1. 内存泄漏风险

| 文件位置 | 问题描述 | 严重程度 |
|---------|---------|---------|
| `useTheme.ts:55` | `mediaQuery.addEventListener` 未在组件卸载时移除 | **高** |
| `frontend-game.vue:197` | `setInterval` 已在 `onUnmounted` 清理 ✅ | - |
| `BackToTop.vue:48-50` | 正确清理事件监听器 ✅ | - |
| `Navbar.vue:102-104` | 正确清理事件监听器 ✅ | - |

---

### 2. 错误处理不当

| 文件位置 | 问题描述 | 严重程度 |
|---------|---------|---------|
| `index-client.ts:26-57` | `checkStatus` 函数对非200状态码统一返回 `-404`，信息不准确 | **中** |
| `index-client.ts:66-75` | 错误码处理直接重定向，丢失错误上下文 | **中** |
| `frontend-ai.vue:280-289` | 错误信息直接展示给用户，可能泄露敏感信息 | **低** |

---

### 3. 性能问题

| 文件位置 | 问题描述 | 严重程度 |
|---------|---------|---------|
| `frontend-game.vue:174-189` | `step()` 函数每次遍历所有单元格并调用 `neighbours()` 多次，O(n²) 复杂度 | **中** |
| `MarkdownRenderer.vue:23-57` | 每次渲染都重新解析markdown，无缓存机制 | **低** |

---

### 4. 状态管理问题

| 文件位置 | 问题描述 | 严重程度 |
|---------|---------|---------|
| `use-global-store.ts:45` | `globalStoreWithout()` 使用 `piniaInit` 但未检查是否已初始化 | **低** |
| `chat.ts:6` | 聊天消息存储在内存中，页面刷新后丢失 | **低** |

---

## 三、UI/UX问题 🟢

### 1. 可访问性问题

| 文件位置 | 问题描述 | 严重程度 |

## 四、第三方依赖安全

建议运行 `npm audit` 检查已知漏洞。发现以下潜在风险：

| 依赖 | 版本 | 风险 |
|-----|-----|-----|
| `axios` | 1.7.2 | 需关注 SSRF 相关配置 |
| `prismjs` | 1.29.0 | 历史存在XSS漏洞，确保最新 |
| `dompurify` | 3.3.2 | 已安装，建议在所有 `v-html` 处使用 |

---

## 五、优先修复建议

1. **立即修复**：所有 `v-html` 使用 `DOMPurify.sanitize()` 消毒
2. **高优先级**：Cookie 设置 `HttpOnly`、`Secure`、`SameSite` 属性（需后端配合）
3. **中优先级**：`useTheme.ts` 事件监听器清理
4. **低优先级**：添加表单loading状态和可访问性标签

<path>C:\Users\zm\Desktop\project\vue3-vite-express\blog-api-ts\src\middlewares\is-admin.ts</path>
<type>file</type>
<content>1: import type { NextFunction } from 'express'
2: import { checkJWT } from '../utils/check-jwt'
3: import type { Req, Res } from '@/types'
4: 
5: /**
6:  * 中间件函数，用于校验用户是否通过登录验证。
7:  *
8:  * @param req 请求对象，包含HTTP请求的相关信息。
9:  * @param res 响应对象，用于发送HTTP响应。
10:  * @param next 一个函数，如果用户通过验证，则调用该函数继续处理请求链。
11:  */
12: export default async (req: Req, res: Res, next: NextFunction) => {
13:     // 尝试从cookie和请求头中获取用户信息
14:     const b_user: string = req.cookies.b_user || req.headers.buser || ''
15:     const b_userid: string = req.cookies.b_userid || req.headers.buserid || ''
16:     const b_username: string = req.cookies.b_username || req.headers.busername || ''
17: 
18:     if (b_user) {
19:         // 如果存在用户信息，尝试验证JWT
20:         const check = await checkJWT(b_user, b_userid, b_username, 'admin')
21:         if (check) {
22:             // 验证通过，继续处理请求
23:             next()
24:         }
25:         else {
26:             // 验证失败，清除cookie并返回错误信息
27:             res.cookie('b_user', '', { maxAge: 0 })
28:             res.cookie('b_userid', '', { maxAge: 0 })
29:             res.cookie('b_username', '', { maxAge: 0 })
30: 
31:             return res.json({
32:                 code: -500,
33:                 message: '登录验证失败',
34:                 data: '',
35:             })
36:         }
37:     }
38:     else {
39:         // 未发现用户信息，直接返回错误信息
40:         return res.json({
41:             code: -500,
42:             message: '请先登录',
43:             data: '',
44:         })
45:     }
46: }

(End of file - total 46 lines)

<content>1: import type { NextFunction } from 'express'
2: import { checkJWT } from '../utils/check-jwt'
3: import type { Req, Res } from '@/types'
4: 
5: /**
6:  * 中间件函数，用于校验用户是否登录。
7:  * 它首先尝试从cookie或header中读取用户信息，然后通过JWT进行验证。
8:  * 如果验证失败或没有提供用户信息，则要求用户重新登录。
9:  *
10:  * @param req 请求对象，包含用户提交的cookies和headers信息。
11:  * @param res 响应对象，用于设置cookie或返回响应数据。
12:  * @param next 用于传递控制权到下一个中间件或路由处理函数。
13:  * @returns 如果验证成功，则调用next()继续处理请求；否则，返回登录验证失败或请先登录的响应。
14:  */
15: export default async (req: Req, res: Res, next: NextFunction) => {
16:     // 尝试从cookie和header中获取用户信息
17:     const user: string = req.cookies.user || req.headers.user || ''
18:     const userid: string = req.cookies.userid || req.headers.userid || ''
19:     const username: string = req.cookies.username || req.headers.username || ''
20: 
21:     if (user) {
22:         // 如果存在用户信息，尝试验证JWT
23:         const check = await checkJWT(user, userid, username, 'user')
24:         if (check) {
25:             // 验证通过，继续处理请求
26:             next()
27:         }
28:         else {
29:             // 验证失败，清除用户cookie并返回错误响应
30:             res.cookie('user', '', { maxAge: 0 })
31:             res.cookie('userid', '', { maxAge: 0 })
32:             res.cookie('username', '', { maxAge: 0 })
33:             res.cookie('useremail', '', { maxAge: 0 })
34:             return res.json({
35:                 code: -400,
36:                 message: '登录验证失败',
37:                 data: '',
38:             })
39:         }
40:     }
41:     else {
42:         // 未提供用户信息，返回需要登录的响应
43:         return res.json({
44:             code: -400,
45:             message: '请先登录',
46:             data: '',
47:         })
48:     }
49: }

<path>C:\Users\zm\Desktop\project\vue3-vite-express\blog-api-ts\src\utils\check-jwt.ts</path>
<type>file</type>
<content>1: import jwt from 'jsonwebtoken'
2: import { secretClient, secretServer } from '../config'
3: 
4: /**
5:  * 检查JWT（JSON Web Token）的有效性。
6:  * @param token 需要验证的JWT字符串。
7:  * @param userid 需要验证的用户ID。
8:  * @param username 需要验证的用户名，将进行解码和比对。
9:  * @param type 标记JWT的类型，决定使用哪个密钥进行验证，'user' 表示用户类型。
10:  * @returns 返回一个Promise，解析为一个布尔值，true表示验证成功，false表示验证失败。
11:  */
12: export function checkJWT(token: string, userid: string, username: string, type: string): Promise<boolean> {
13:     return new Promise((resolve) => {
14:         // 根据JWT类型选择使用的密钥
15:         const secret = type === 'user' ? secretClient : secretServer
16:         jwt.verify(token, secret, (err, decoded) => {
17:             // 验证出现错误，或者解码结果为空或为字符串，认为验证失败
18:             if (err || !decoded || typeof decoded === 'string') {
19:                 resolve(false)
20:             }
21:             // 检查解码后的id和username是否匹配
22:             else if (decoded.id === userid && (decoded.username === username || decoded.username === encodeURI(username))) {
23:                 resolve(true)
24:             }
25:             // 不匹配，验证失败
26:             else {
27:                 resolve(false)
28:             }
29:         })
30:     })
31: }

(End of file - total 31 lines)
</content>
```

<content>1: import fs from 'node:fs'
2: import md5 from 'md5'
3: import jwt from 'jsonwebtoken'
4: 
5: import { fsExistsSync, getErrorMessage, getNowTime } from '../utils'
6: import { md5Pre, secretServer as secret } from '../config'
7: import AdminM from '../models/admin'
8: import type { Lists, ResData, User, UserModify } from '@/types'
9: 
10: /**
11:  * 获取管理员列表
12:  */
13: export async function getList(reqQuery: { page?: number; limit?: number }) {
14:     let json: ResData<Nullable<Lists<User[]>>>
15: 
16:     const sort = '-_id'
17:     const page = Number(reqQuery.page) || 1
18:     const limit = Number(reqQuery.limit) || 10
19:     const skip = (page - 1) * limit
20:     try {
21:         const [list, total] = await Promise.all([
22:             AdminM.find().sort(sort).skip(skip).limit(limit).exec().then(data => data.map(item => item.toObject())),
23:             AdminM.countDocuments(),
24:         ])
25:         const totalPage = Math.ceil(total / limit)
26:         json = {
27:             code: 200,
28:             data: {
29:                 list,
30:                 total,
31:                 hasNext: totalPage > page ? 1 : 0,
32:                 hasPrev: page > 1 ? 1 : 0,
33:             },
34:         }
35:     }
36:     catch (err: unknown) {
37:         json = { code: -200, data: null, message: getErrorMessage(err) }
38:     }
39: 
40:     return json
41: }
42: 
43: /**
44:  * 获取单个管理员
45:  */
46: export async function getItem(reqQuery: { id: string }) {
47:     let json: ResData<Nullable<User>>
48: 
49:     const {
50:         id: _id,
51:     } = reqQuery
52: 
53:     if (!_id) {
54:         json = { code: -200, data: null, message: '参数错误' }
55:     }
56:     else {
57:         try {
58:             const filter = { _id }
59:             const result = await AdminM.findOne(filter).exec().then(data => data?.toObject())
60:             json = { code: 200, data: result, message: 'success' }
61:         }
62:         catch (err: unknown) {
63:             json = { code: -200, data: null, message: getErrorMessage(err) }
64:         }
65:     }
66: 
67:     return json
68: }
69: 
70: /**
71:  * 管理员登录
72:  */
73: export async function login(reqBody: { password: string; username: string }) {
74:     let json: ResData<{ userid: string; user: string; username: string } | null>
75: 
76:     const {
77:         password,
78:         username,
79:     } = reqBody
80: 
81:     if (username === '' || password === '') {
82:         json = { code: -200, data: null, message: '请输入用户名和密码' }
83:     }
84:     else {
85:         try {
86:             const filter = {
87:                 username,
88:                 password: md5(md5Pre + password),
89:                 is_delete: 0,
90:             }
91:             const result = await AdminM.findOne(filter).exec().then(data => data?.toObject())
92:             if (result) {
93:                 const _username = encodeURI(username)
94:                 const id = result.id || ''
95:                 const token = jwt.sign({ id, username: _username }, secret, { expiresIn: 60 * 60 * 24 * 30 })
96: 
97:                 json = {
98:                     code: 200,
99:                     message: '登录成功',
100:                     data: {
101:                         user: token,
102:                         username: _username,
103:                         userid: id,
104:                     },
105:                 }
106:             }
107:             else {
108:                 json = { code: -200, data: null, message: '用户名或者密码错误' }
109:             }
110:         }
111:         catch (err: unknown) {
112:             json = { code: -200, data: null, message: getErrorMessage(err) }
113:         }
114:     }
115: 
116:     return json
117: }
118: 
119: /**
120:  * 初始化时添加管理员
121:  */
122: export async function insert(email: string, password: string, username: string) {
123:     let message = ''
124: 
125:     if (fsExistsSync('./admin.lock')) {
126:         message = '请先把项目根目录的 admin.lock 文件删除'
127:     }
128:     else if (!username || !password || !email) {
129:         message = '请将表单填写完整'
130:     }
131:     else {
132:         try {
133:             const filter = { username }
134:             const result = await AdminM.findOne(filter).exec().then(data => data?.toObject())
135:             if (result) {
136:                 message = `${username}: 已经存在`
137:             }
138:             else {
139:                 const body = {
140:                     username,
141:                     password: md5(md5Pre + password),
142:                     email,
143:                     creat_date: getNowTime(),
144:                     update_date: getNowTime(),
145:                     is_delete: 0,
146:                     timestamp: getNowTime('X'),
147:                 }
148:                 await AdminM.create(body)
149:                 fs.writeFileSync('./admin.lock', username)
150:                 message = `添加用户成功: ${username}, 密码: ${password}`
151:             }
152:         }
153:         catch (err: unknown) {
154:             message = getErrorMessage(err)
155:         }
156:     }
157:     return message
158: }
159: 
160: /**
161:  * 管理员编辑
162:  */
163: export async function modify(reqBody: { id: string; email: string; password: string; username: string }) {
164:     let json: ResData<Nullable<User>>
165: 
166:     const {
167:         id: _id,
168:         email,
169:         password,
170:         username,
171:     } = reqBody
172: 
173:     const body: UserModify = {
174:         email,
175:         username,
176:         update_date: getNowTime(),
177:     }
178:     if (password) {
179:         body.password = md5(md5Pre + password)
180:     }
181: 
182:     try {
183:         const filter = { _id }
184:         const result = await AdminM.findOneAndUpdate(filter, body, { new: true }).exec().then(data => data?.toObject())
185:         json = { code: 200, message: '更新成功', data: result }
186:     }
187:     catch (err: unknown) {
188:         json = { code: -200, data: null, message: getErrorMessage(err) }
189:     }
190: 
191:     return json
192: }
193: 
194: /**
195:  * 管理员删除
196:  */
197: export async function deletes(reqQuery: { id: string }) {
198:     let json: ResData<string | null>
199: 
200:     const {
201:         id: _id,
202:     } = reqQuery
203: 
204:     try {
205:         const filter = { _id }
206:         const body = { is_delete: 1 }
207:         await AdminM.updateOne(filter, body).exec()
208:         json = { code: 200, message: '删除成功', data: 'success' }
209:     }
210:     catch (err: unknown) {
211:         json = { code: -200, data: null, message: getErrorMessage(err) }
212:     }
213: 
214:     return json
215: }
216: 
217: /**
218:  * 管理员恢复
219:  */
220: export async function recover(reqQuery: { id: string }) {
221:     let json: ResData<string | null>
222: 
223:     const {
224:         id: _id,
225:     } = reqQuery
226: 
227:     try {
228:         const filter = { _id }
229:         const body = { is_delete: 0 }
230:         await AdminM.updateOne(filter, body).exec()
231:         json = { code: 200, message: '恢复成功', data: 'success' }
232:     }
233:     catch (err: unknown) {
234:         json = { code: -200, data: null, message: getErrorMessage(err) }
235:     }
236: 
237:     return json
238: }

35: export async function jscodeToSession(req: Req<object, { js_code: string }>, res: Res) {

46:     res.json(await helper.wxLogin(reqBody))
47: }

50:  * 用户退出

54: export function logout(req: Req, res: Res) {
55:     const json = helper.logout()
56: 
57:     res.cookie('user', '', { maxAge: -1 })
58:     res.cookie('userid', '', { maxAge: -1 })
59:     res.cookie('username', '', { maxAge: -1 })
60:     res.cookie('useremail', '', { maxAge: -1 })
61:

2: import hljs from 'highlight.js'
3: 
4: import ArticleM from '../models/article'
5: import CategoryM from '../models/category'
6: import { getErrorMessage, getNowTime } from '../utils'
7: import type { Article, ArticleInsert, ArticleModify, Lists, ResData } from '@/types'

9: /**
10:  * 将 Markdown 格式的内容转换成 HTML 格式，并生成目录（TOC）。
11:  * @param content Markdown格式的字符串。
12:  * @returns 返回一个对象，包含生成的 HTML 和 TOC。
13:  */
14: function marked(content: string) {
15:     // 初始化返回对象，包含 html 和 toc 两个属性
16:     const $return = {
17:         html: '',
18:         toc: '',
19:     }
20: 
21:     // 使用 markdownIt 库将 Markdown 内容渲染为 HTML
22:     const html = markdownIt({
23:         breaks: true, // 启用换行符转换
24:         html: true, // 允许 HTML 标签
25:         linkify: true, // 自动转换 URL 为链接
26:         typographer: true, // 启用更美观的排版
27:         highlight(str, lang) {
28:             // 高亮代码块
29:             if (lang && hljs.getLanguage(lang)) {
30:                 try {
31:                     return hljs.highlight(lang, str).value
32:                 }
33:                 catch (error) {} // 捕获并忽略高亮过程中的错误
34:             }
35:             return ''
36:         },
37:     }).render(content)
38: 
39:     // 将渲染后的 HTML 存储到返回对象中
40:     $return.html = html
41: 
42:     // 返回包含 HTML 和 TOC 的对象
43:     return $return
44: }
45: 
46: /**
47:  * 获取文章列表的异步函数。
48:  */
49: export async function getList(reqQuery: { page: string; limit: string; sort: string }) {
50:     let json: ResData<Nullable<Lists<Article[]>>>
51: 
52:     // 处理查询参数，设定默认值
53:     const sort = reqQuery.sort || '-update_date'
54:     const page = Number(reqQuery.page) || 1
55:     const limit = Number(reqQuery.limit) || 15
56:     const skip = (page - 1) * limit
57: 
58:     try {
59:         // 同时查询文章列表和总数，计算总页数
60:         const [list, total] = await Promise.all([
61:             ArticleM.find().sort(sort).skip(skip).limit(limit).exec().then(data => data.map(item => item.toObject())),
62:             ArticleM.countDocuments(),
63:         ])
64:         const totalPage = Math.ceil(total / limit)
65:         // 构建响应数据对象
66:         json = {
67:             code: 200,
68:             data: {
69:                 list,
70:                 total,
71:                 hasNext: totalPage > page ? 1 : 0,
72:                 hasPrev: page > 1 ? 1 : 0,
73:             },
74:             message: 'success',
75:         }
76:     }
77:     catch (err: unknown) {
78:         // 捕获异常，返回错误信息
79:         json = { code: -200, data: null, message: getErrorMessage(err) }
80:     }
81: 
82:     return json
83: }
84: 
85: /**

88: export async function getItem(reqQuery: { id: string }) {

93:         id: _id,
94:     } = reqQuery

100:     }
101:     else {

104:             const filter = { _id }

107:             // 查询成功，返回文章详情
108:             json = { code: 200, message: 'success', data: result }
109:         }
110:         catch (err: unknown) {

113:         }

120: /**
121:  * 异步插入文章。
122:  */
123: export async function insert(reqBody: ArticleInsert) {
124:     let json: ResData<Nullable<Article>>
125: 
126:     // 从请求体中解构文章信息
127:     const {
128:         category,
129:         content,
130:         title,
131:         html,
132:     } = reqBody
133: 
134:     // 根据是否提供html，处理markdown内容
135:     let mdHtml: string, mdToc: string
136:     if (html) {
137:         mdHtml = html
138:         mdToc = ''
139:     }
140:     else {
141:         // 如果没有提供html，则使用marked库处理markdown内容生成html和toc
142:         const md = marked(content)
143:         mdToc = md.toc
144:         mdHtml = md.html
145:     }
146: 
147:     // 处理文章分类，将其拆分为id和名称
148:     const arr_category = category.split('|')
149:     const data: Article = {
150:         title,
151:         category: arr_category[0],
152:         category_name: arr_category[1],
153:         content,
154:         html: mdHtml,
155:         toc: mdToc,
156:         visit: 0,
157:         like: 0,
158:         comment_count: 0,
159:         creat_date: getNowTime(),
160:         update_date: getNowTime(),
161:         is_delete: 0,
162:         timestamp: getNowTime('X'),
163:     }
164:     try {
165:         // 创建文章，并在创建成功后更新分类数量
166:         const result = await ArticleM.create(data).then(data => data.toObject())
167: 
168:         const filter = { _id: arr_category[0] }
169:         const body = {
170:             $inc: {
171:                 cate_num: 1,
172:             },
173:         }
174:         await CategoryM.updateOne(filter, body).exec()
175:         // 返回成功响应
176:         json = { code: 200, message: '发布成功', data: result }
177:     }
178:     catch (err: unknown) {
179:         // 捕获错误，返回错误响应
180:         json = { code: -200, data: null, message: getErrorMessage(err) }
181:     }
182: 
183:     return json
184: }
185: 
186: /**
187:  * 删除文章记录及其对应分类的数量减一。

81:         const client = new AipImageClassifyClient(shihuaConfig.APP_ID, shihuaConfig.API_KEY, shihuaConfig.SECRET_KEY)

84:             const image = await getBase64(img_id, cdn)

86:             if (image) {
87:                 const options: Objable = {}
88:                 options.baike_num = '5'
89:                 // 带参数调用植物识别
90:                 console.log(`识图开始时间:${new Date().getTime()}`)
91:                 const shihuaResult = await client.plantDetect(image, options)
92:                 console.log(`识图结束时间:${new Date().getTime()}`)

96:                         let img, name

99: 
100:                             if (item.baike_info && item.baike_info.image_url) {
101:                                 name = item.name
102:                                 img = item.baike_info.image_url
103:                                 break
104:                             }
105:                         }
106:                         if (cdn === 'qiniu') {
107:                             img = `${cdnDomain}app/${img_id}`
108:                         }
109:                         else {
110:                             img = `${domain}uploads/${img_id}`
111:                         }
112:

121:                                 is_delete: 0,

123:                             })
124:                             // fs.unlinkSync('./uploads/' + img_id)
125:                         }
126:                     }
127:                     return {
128:                         success: true,
129:                         data: shihuaResult,
130:                     }
131:                 }
132:                 return {
133:                     success: false,
134:                     err: 'shitu',
135:                     message: shihuaResult.error_msg,
136:                 }
137:             }
138:             return {
139:                 success: false,
140:                 err: 'down-img',
141:                 message: '图片读取失败',
142:             }
143:         }
144:         catch (err: unknown) {
145:             return { success: false, err: 'unknow', message: getErrorMessage(err) }
146:         }
147:     }
148: 
149:     try {
150:         const filter = { img_id }
151:         const result = await ShiHuaM.findOne(filter).then(data => data?.toObject())
152:         if (result) {
153:             res.json({
154:                 code: 200,
155:                 from: 'db',
156:                 userid,
157:                 result: JSON.parse(result.result),
158:             })
159:         }
160:         else {
161:             let data = await getData()
162:             if (!data.success && data.err === 'unknow') {
163:                 data = await getData()
164:             }
165:             if (!data.success && data.err === 'unknow') {
166:                 data = await getData()
167:             }
168:             if (data.success) {
169:                 res.json({ code: 200, from: 'api', userid, ...data.data })
170:             }
171:             else {
172:                 res.json({ code: -200, userid, message: data.message || '读取数据失败' })
173:             }
174:         }
175:     }
176:     catch (err: unknown) {

178:     }
179: }

182:  * 获取识花历史列表
183:  * @param req - 请求对象，包含查询参数和请求头
184:  * @param res - 响应对象，用于返回操作结果
185:  */
186: export async function getHistory(req: Req<{ page?: number; limit?: number }>, res: Res) {
187:     let json: ResData<Nullable<Lists<ShiHua[]>>>
188:     const reqQuery = req.query
189: 
190:     const userid = req.cookies.userid || req.headers.userid
191: 
192:     const {
193:         page = 1,
194:         limit = 10,
195:     } = reqQuery
196: 
197:     const payload = {
198:         is_delete: 0,
199:         user_id: userid,
200:     }

202:     const sort = '-creat_date'
203: 
204:     try {
205:         const [data, total] = await Promise.all([

207:             ShiHuaM.countDocuments(payload),
208:         ])
209:         const totalPage = Math.ceil(total / limit)
210:         json = {
211:             code: 200,
212:             data: {
213:                 list: data.map((item) => {
214:                     item.result = ''
215:                     return item
216:                 }),
217:                 total,
218:                 hasNext: totalPage > page ? 1 : 0,
219:                 hasPrev: page > 1 ? 1 : 0,
220:             },
221:         }
222:     }
223:     catch (err: unknown) {
224:         json = { code: -200, data: null, message: getErrorMessage(err) }
225:     }
226: 
227:     res.json(json)
228: }
229:

231:  * 删除识花历史列表
232:  * @method delHistory

16: 
17:     const creat_date = getNowTime()
18:     const timestamp = getNowTime('X')
19:     if (!_id) {
20:         json = { code: -200, data: null, message: '参数错误' }
21:     }
22:     else if (!content) {
23:         json = { code: -200, data: null, message: '请输入评论内容' }
24:     }
25:     else if (!userid) {
26:         json = { code: -200, data: null, message: '请先登录' }
27:     }
28:     else {
29:         const data: Comment = {
30:             article_id: _id,
31:             userid,
32:             content,
33:             creat_date,
34:             is_delete: 0,
35:             timestamp,
36:         }
37:         try {
38:             const result = await CommentM.create(data).then(data => data.toObject())
39:             const filter = { _id }
40:             const body = {
41:                 $inc: {
42:                     comment_count: 1,
43:                 },
44:             }
45:             await ArticleM.updateOne(filter, body).exec()
46:             json = { code: 200, data: result, message: '发布成功' }
47:         }
48:         catch (err: unknown) {
49:             json = { code: -200, data: null, message: getErrorMessage(err) }
50:         }
51:     }
52: 
53:     return json
54: }
55: 
56: /**
57:  * 前台浏览时, 读取评论列表
58:  */
59: export async function getList(reqQuery: ReqListQuery) {
60:     let json: ResData<Nullable<Lists<Comment[]>>>
61: 
62:     const {
63:         all,
64:         id: article_id,
65:     } = reqQuery
66: 
67:     let { limit, page } = reqQuery
68: 
69:     if (!article_id) {
70:         json = { code: -200, data: null, message: '参数错误' }
71:     }
72:     else {
73:         page = Number(page) || 1
74:         limit = Number(limit) || 10
75: 
76:         const data: {
77:             article_id: string
78:             is_delete?: number
79:         } = {
80:             article_id,
81:         }
82:         const skip = (page - 1) * limit
83:         if (!all) {
84:             data.is_delete = 0
85:         }
86: 
87:         try {
88:             const [list, total] = await Promise.all([
89:                 CommentM.find(data).sort('-_id').skip(skip).limit(limit).exec().then(data => data.map(item => item.toObject())),
90:                 CommentM.countDocuments(data),
91:             ])
92:             const totalPage = Math.ceil(total / limit)
93:             json = {
94:                 code: 200,
95:                 data: {
96:                     list,
97:                     total,
98:                     hasNext: totalPage > page ? 1 : 0,
99:                     hasPrev: page > 1 ? 1 : 0,
100:                 },
101:             }
102:         }
103:         catch (err: unknown) {
104:             json = { code: -200, data: null, message: getErrorMessage(err) }
105:         }
106:     }
107: 
108:     return json
109: }
110: 
111: /**
112:  * 评论删除
113:  */
114: export async function deletes(reqQuery: { id: string }) {
115:     let json: ResData<string | null>
116: 
117:     const {
118:         id: _id,
119:     } = reqQuery

121:     try {

125:         await Promise.all([
126:             CommentM.updateOne(filter, commentBody).exec(),
127:             ArticleM.updateOne(filter, ArticleBody).exec(),
128:         ])
129:         json = { code: 200, message: '删除成功', data: 'success' }
130:     }
131:     catch (err: unknown) {
132:         json = { code: -200, data: null, message: getErrorMessage(err) }
133:     }

136: }

141:                 .filter(item => item.itemid !== ''),
142:         })

153:  * @returns void

155: export async function user(req: Req<{ containerid: string; since_id: string }>, res: Res) {
156:     const reqQuery = req.query
157: 
158:     const containerid = reqQuery.containerid
159:     const since_id = reqQuery.since_id
160:     if (!containerid) {

162:         return

165:         ...baseOptions,

167:     }

171:         const list: any[] = []

现在我已经完成了全面的代码审查。以下是详细的安全问题报告：

---

# blog-api-ts 安全漏洞深度检查报告

## 🔴 严重

### 1. 硬编码 API 密钥
**文件**: `src/config/index.ts:28`
```typescript
export const DS_API_KEY = process.env.DS_API_KEY || 'sk-sp-14e207d3d0724c868b4ec7ed724f35e2'
```
**问题**: 默认 API Key 硬编码在源码中，如果环境变量未设置将暴露密钥。
**修复**: 移除默认值，强制要求环境变量配置。

---

### 2. JWT Secret 使用弱密钥生成
**文件**: `src/init.ts:14-18`
```typescript
const secretServer1 = Math.random() * 1000000
const secretClient1 = Math.random() * 1000000
```
**问题**: `Math.random()` 不安全，生成的密钥可预测且只有 6 位数字。
**修复**: 使用 `crypto.randomBytes(64)` 生成强密钥。

---

### 3. Cookie 安全配置缺失
**文件**: `src/api/backend-user.ts:42-44`, `src/api/frontend-user.ts:21-25`
```typescript
res.cookie('b_user', json.data.user, { maxAge: remember_me })
```
**问题**: Cookie 未设置 `httpOnly`, `secure`, `sameSite` 属性。
**修复**:
```typescript
res.cookie('b_user', token, {
    maxAge: remember_me,
    httpOnly: true,
    secure: process.env.NODE_ENV === 'production',
    sameSite: 'strict'
})
```

---

### 4. CORS 配置过于宽松
**文件**: `src/middlewares/cors.ts:14`
```typescript
res.header('Access-Control-Allow-Origin', '*')
```
**问题**: 允许所有来源访问，容易遭受 CSRF 攻击。
**修复**: 使用白名单配置允许的域名。

---

### 5. 管理员添加接口无保护
**文件**: `src/routes/index.ts:8-15`
```typescript
router.post('/', async (req, res) => {
    const { email, password, username } = req.body
    const message = await backendUser.insert(email, password, username)
})
```
**问题**: `/backend/` 路由添加管理员，虽然有 `admin.lock` 文件保护，但仅删除文件即可绕过。
**修复**: 
- 添加首次安装检测
- 移除或禁用此路由
- 使用 CLI 工具创建管理员

---

### 6. SQL/NoSQL 注入风险
**文件**: 多个文件中的数据库查询直接使用用户输入

- `src/api/backend-article.helper.ts:104` - 直接使用 `_id`
- `src/api/backend-user.helper.ts:58` - 直接使用 `_id`
- `src/api/frontend-user.helper.ts:258` - 直接使用 `userid`

**问题**: 未验证 ID 格式，可能被利用进行 NoSQL 注入。
**修复**: 使用 mongoose 的 `Types.ObjectId.isValid()` 验证 ID 格式。

---

## 🟠 高危

### 7. 文件上传安全漏洞
**文件**: `src/app/app-shihua.ts:14-23`
```typescript
const storage = multer.diskStorage({
    destination(_req, _file, cb) {
        cb(null, './uploads')
    },
    filename(_req, file, cb) {
        const ext = file.originalname.split('.').pop()
        cb(null, `shihua-${Date.now()}.${ext}`)
    },
})
```
**问题**:
- 无文件类型验证
- 无文件大小限制
- 文件扩展名直接来自用户输入
- 无病毒扫描

**修复**:
```typescript
const ALLOWED_TYPES = ['image/jpeg', 'image/png', 'image/gif']
const MAX_SIZE = 10 * 1024 * 1024

const upload = multer({
    storage,
    fileFilter: (req, file, cb) => {
        if (!ALLOWED_TYPES.includes(file.mimetype)) {
            return cb(new Error('不支持的文件类型'))
        }
        cb(null, true)
    },
    limits: { fileSize: MAX_SIZE }
})
```

---

### 8. 密码哈希使用 MD5
**文件**: `src/api/backend-user.helper.ts:88`, `src/api/frontend-user.helper.ts:66`
```typescript
password: md5(md5Pre + password)
```
**问题**: MD5 已被证明不安全，且仅使用简单前缀的盐值。
**修复**: 使用 `bcrypt` 或 `argon2`。

---

### 9. XSS 跨站脚本攻击风险
**文件**: `src/api/backend-article.helper.ts:22-37`
```typescript
const html = markdownIt({
    breaks: true,
    html: true,  // 允许 HTML 标签
    ...
}).render(content)
```
**问题**: Markdown 渲染允许原始 HTML，可能导致 XSS。
**修复**: 使用 `DOMPurify` 清理 HTML，或禁用 `html: true`。

---

### 10. 未授权 API 接口暴露
**文件**: `src/routes/app.ts`
```typescript
router.post('/douyin/user/insert', cors, appDouYin.insertUser)  // 无认证
router.post('/douyin/insert', cors, appDouYin.insert)           // 无认证
router.post('/chat/completions', cors, chatCompletions)         // 无认证
router.get('/qiniu/token', cors, appQiniu.token)                // 无认证
```
**问题**: 多个 API 无认证保护，任何人可调用。
**修复**: 添加认证中间件或速率限制。

---

### 11. 请求体大小限制过大
**文件**: `src/app.ts:76,82`
```typescript
app.use(express.json({ limit: '50mb' }))
app.use(express.urlencoded({ limit: '50mb', extended: true }))
```
**问题**: 50MB 限制过大，可能导致 DoS 攻击。
**修复**: 根据实际需求设置合理限制（如 1-5MB）。

---

### 12. 硬编码第三方 Cookie/Token
**文件**: `src/app/app-weibo.ts:39`
```typescript
'cookie': 'SCF=Aip1F5fqYgfG7nzFqjK3Umxcyp0ztYFLhFYqAAQMvjFPG0UhUj0fJHdp0A7j7wfLwTXfaHg_dOII1ioFQajhYGE.; ...'
```
**问题**: 硬编码的微博 Cookie 可能失效且存在安全风险。
**修复**: 从环境变量读取或使用 OAuth 认证。

---

## 🟡 中危

### 13. 缺少速率限制
**文件**: `src/app.ts`
**问题**: 无登录、注册等敏感操作的速率限制，易受暴力破解攻击。
**修复**: 使用 `express-rate-limit` 中间件。

---

### 14. 敏感信息泄露
**文件**: `src/api/backend-user.helper.ts:150`
```typescript
message = `添加用户成功: ${username}, 密码: ${password}`
```
**问题**: 返回明文密码。
**修复**: 移除密码显示。

---

### 15. JWT 过期时间过长
**文件**: `src/api/backend-user.helper.ts:95`, `src/api/frontend-user.helper.ts:77`
```typescript
{ expiresIn: 60 * 60 * 24 * 30 }  // 30 天
```
**问题**: Token 有效期过长，增加被盗用风险。
**修复**: 缩短有效期（如 1-24 小时），使用 Refresh Token 机制。

---

### 16. 错误信息泄露内部细节
**文件**: `src/app.ts:140`
```typescript
message: process.env.NODE_ENV === 'production' ? '服务器内部错误' : err.message
```
**问题**: 开发环境泄露错误堆栈。
**修复**: 生产环境统一返回通用错误信息。

---

### 17. 缺少输入验证库
**问题**: 所有输入验证都是手动编写，不完整且容易遗漏。
**修复**: 使用 `joi`, `zod` 或 `class-validator` 进行统一验证。

---

### 18. HTTP 安全头缺失
**文件**: `src/app.ts`
**问题**: 缺少 `helmet` 中间件设置安全头。
**修复**:
```typescript
import helmet from 'helmet'
app.use(helmet())
```

---

### 19. 日志中可能包含敏感信息
**文件**: `src/app/chat-helper.ts:63,83`
```typescript
console.log('Chat request:', { model: requestBody.model, stream: isStream, messagesCount: requestBody.messages.length })
```
**问题**: 生产环境日志可能泄露敏感信息。
**修复**: 使用专业日志库（如 `winston`、`pino`），脱敏处理。

---

### 20. 路径遍历风险
**文件**: `src/app/app-shihua.ts:245`
```typescript
fs.unlinkSync(`./uploads/${img_id}`)
```
**问题**: `img_id` 未验证，可能导致路径遍历删除任意文件。
**修复**: 验证文件名格式，使用 `path.basename()`。

---

## 🔵 低危

### 21. 第三方依赖风险
**文件**: `package.json`
- `md5@2.3.0` - 已弃用，使用不安全的 MD5
- `connect-multiparty@2.2.0` - 已弃用，建议使用 `multer`
- `base64-img@1.0.4` - 可能有安全问题

**修复**: 更新依赖，替换不安全包。

---

### 22. 调试代码未移除
**文件**: 多处 `console.log` 语句
**修复**: 使用条件日志或移除。

---

### 23. MongoDB 连接无认证
**文件**: `src/mongoose.ts:7`
```typescript
mongoose.connect(mongoUri, {})  // 无认证选项
```
**修复**: 生产环境启用认证。

---

103: <script lang="ts" setup>

115: interface Message {
116:     role: 'user' | 'assistant'
117:     content: string
118:     timestamp: Date
119: }
120: 
121: interface Model {
122:     id: string
123:     name: string
124: }
125: 
126: // Coding Plan 支持的模型列表（阿里云 DashScope）
127: const modelList: Model[] = [
128:     { id: 'qwen3.5-plus', name: '千问 3.5 Plus' },
129:     { id: 'qwen3-max-2026-01-23', name: '千问 3 Max' },
130:     { id: 'qwen3-coder-next', name: '千问 3 Coder Next' },

134:     { id: 'kimi-k2.5', name: 'Kimi K2.5' },
135:     { id: 'MiniMax-M2.5', name: 'MiniMax M2.5' },
136: ]
137: 
138: const selectedModelId = ref<string>(modelList[0].id)
139: const modelName = computed(() => {
140:     const found = modelList.find(item => item.id === selectedModelId.value)
141:     return found?.name || selectedModelId.value
142: })
143: 
144: const messages = ref<Message[]>([])
145: const userInput = ref('')
146: const isLoading = ref(false)
147: const enableThinking = ref(false)
148: 
149: const scrollToBottom = async () => {
150:     await nextTick()
151:     const messagesArea = document.querySelector('.messages-area')
152:     if (messagesArea) {
153:         messagesArea.scrollTop = messagesArea.scrollHeight
154:     }
155: }
156: 
157: const formatTime = (date: Date) => {
158:     return date.toLocaleTimeString('zh-CN', {
159:         hour: '2-digit',
160:         minute: '2-digit'
161:     })
162: }
163: 
164: // 处理 <think>...</think> 标签，将推理内容显示为小字
165: const processThinkContent = (content: string): string => {
166:     const thinkMatch = content.match(/<think>([\s\S]*?)<\/think>/)
167:     if (thinkMatch) {
168:         const thinkContent = thinkMatch[1]
169:         const smallThinkContent = `<small style="font-size: 0.8em; color: #6b7280;">${thinkContent}</small>`
170:         return content.replace(thinkMatch[0], smallThinkContent)
171:     }
172:     return content
173: }
174: 
175: const processedContent = (content: string): string => {
176:     return processThinkContent(content)
177: }
178: 
179: // 处理推理内容（reasoning_content）
180: const processReasoningContent = (content: string): string => {
181:     return `<small style="font-size: 0.8em; color: #6b7280;">${content}</small>`
182: }
183: 
184: const clearMessages = () => {
185:     messages.value = []
186:     messages.value.push({
187:         role: 'assistant',
188:         content: '你好！我是湛明 AI 助手，有什么可以帮助你的吗？',
189:         timestamp: new Date()
190:     })
191:     ElMessage.success('已开始新对话')
192: }
193: 
194: const sendMessage = async () => {
195:     if (!userInput.value.trim() || isLoading.value) {
196:         return
197:     }
198: 
199:     const userMessage: Message = {
200:         role: 'user',
201:         content: userInput.value.trim(),
202:         timestamp: new Date()
203:     }
204: 
205:     messages.value.push(userMessage)
206:     userInput.value = ''
207:     isLoading.value = true
208: 
209:     await scrollToBottom()
210: 
211:     try {
212:         // 调用后端 API（流式模式）
213:         const response = await fetch('/api/app/chat/completions', {
214:             method: 'POST',
215:             headers: {
216:                 'Content-Type': 'application/json',
217:                 'Accept': 'text/event-stream',
218:             },
219: body: JSON.stringify({
220:                 model: selectedModelId.value,
221:                 messages: messages.value.map(m => ({
222:                     role: m.role,
223:                     content: m.content
224:                 })),
225:                 stream: true,
226:                 thinking: enableThinking.value
227:             })
228:         })
229: 
230:         if (!response.ok) {
231:             const errorData = await response.json().catch(() => ({}))
232:             throw new Error(`API 请求失败：${response.status} - ${errorData.message || response.statusText}`)
233:         }
234: 
235:         // 添加空的 AI 消息容器
236:         const aiMessageIndex = messages.value.length
237:         messages.value.push({
238:             role: 'assistant',
239:             content: '',
240:             timestamp: new Date()
241:         })
242: 
243:         // 处理流式响应
244:         const reader = response.body?.getReader()
245:         if (!reader) {
246:             throw new Error('无法读取响应流')
247:         }
248: 
249:         const decoder = new TextDecoder('utf-8')
250:         let buffer = ''
251: 
252:         while (true) {
253:             const { done, value } = await reader.read()
254:             if (done) break
255: 
256:             buffer += decoder.decode(value, { stream: true })
257:             const lines = buffer.split('\n')
258:             buffer = lines.pop() || ''
259: 
260:             for (const line of lines) {
261:                 const trimmedLine = line.trim()
262:                 if (!trimmedLine || !trimmedLine.startsWith('data:')) continue
263:                 if (trimmedLine === 'data: [DONE]') continue
264: 
265:                 try {
266:                     const json = JSON.parse(trimmedLine.slice(6))
267:                     const delta = json.choices?.[0]?.delta
268: 
269:                     if (delta?.content) {
270:                         messages.value[aiMessageIndex].content += delta.content
271:                         await scrollToBottom()
272:                     }
273:                 }
274:                 catch (e) {
275:                     console.warn('解析 SSE 数据失败:', e)
276:                 }
277:             }
278:         }
279:     }
280:     catch (error) {
281:         console.error('Error sending message:', error)
282:         const errorMessage: Message = {
283:             role: 'assistant',
284:             content: `抱歉，发生了一个错误：${error instanceof Error ? error.message : '未知错误'}`,
285:             timestamp: new Date()
286:         }
287:         messages.value.push(errorMessage)
288:         ElMessage.error('发送消息失败')
289:     }
290:     finally {
291:         isLoading.value = false
292:         await scrollToBottom()
293:     }
294: }
295: 
296: const handleModelChange = (command: string) => {
297:     selectedModelId.value = command
298:     ElMessage.success(`已切换到 ${modelName.value}`)
299: }
300:

  "filePath": "C:\\Users\\zm\\Desktop\\project\\vue3-vite-express\\blog-vite-vue3\\src\\api\\index-client.ts"

<type>file</type>
<content>1: import axios from 'axios'
2: import qs from 'qs'
3: 
4: import type { AxiosResponse } from 'axios'
5: import config from './config-client'
6: 
7: axios.interceptors.request.use(
8:     (config) => {
9:         return config
10:     },
11:     (error) => {
12:         return Promise.reject(error)
13:     },
14: )
15: 
16: axios.interceptors.response.use(
17:     response => response,
18:     error => Promise.resolve(error.response),
19: )
20: 
21: /**
22:  * 检查HTTP响应的状态，并返回处理后的响应数据。
23:  * @param response - AxiosResponse对象，包含从服务器接收的完整响应信息。
24:  * @returns 返回一个ResponseData对象，要么是原始响应数据，要么是包含错误代码、错误消息和空数据的对象。
25:  */
26: function checkStatus(response: AxiosResponse): ResponseData<any> {
27:     // Validate the response object
28:     if (!response) {
29:         return {
30:             code: -404,
31:             message: '未知错误: 响应对象不存在',
32:             data: '',
33:         }
34:     }
35: 
36:     // Validate the response status
37:     if (response.status === 200 || response.status === 304) {
38:         // Validate the response data
39:         if (response.data) {
40:             return response.data
41:         }
42:         else {
43:             return {
44:                 code: -404,
45:                 message: '未知错误: 响应数据不存在',
46:                 data: '',
47:             }
48:         }
49:     }
50: 
51:     // Return an error object with the status text or a default message
52:     return {
53:         code: -404,
54:         message: response.statusText || '未知错误',
55:         data: '',
56:     }
57: }
58: 
59: /**
60:  * 检查响应码并根据不同的响应码执行相应的操作。
61:  * @param res - 包含响应数据和状态码的对象。
62:  * @returns 返回原始的响应对象。
63:  */
64: function checkCode(res: ResponseData<any>): ResponseData<any> {
65:     // 根据不同的响应码重定向到不同的页面或显示消息
66:     if (res.code === -500) {
67:         window.location.href = '/backend'
68:     }
69:     else if (res.code === -400) {
70:         window.location.href = '/'
71:     }
72:     else if (res.code !== 200) {
73:         showMsg(res.message)
74:     }
75:     return res
76: }
77: 
78: /**
79:  * axios Api 封装
80:  * @returns ApiClient
81:  * @example
82:  * ```
83:  * get(url: '/api/url', params: {}, headers: {})
84:  * post(url: '/api/url', data: {}, headers: {})
85:  * file(url: '/api/url', data: {}, headers: {})
86:  * ```
87:  */
88: function api(): ApiClient {
89:     return {
90:         async file(url, data) {
91:             const response = await axios({
92:                 method: 'post',
93:                 url,
94:                 data,
95:                 headers: {
96:                     'X-Requested-With': 'XMLHttpRequest',
97:                 },
98:             })
99:             const res = checkStatus(response)
100:             return checkCode(res)
101:         },
102:         async post(url, data) {
103:             const response = await axios({
104:                 method: 'post',
105:                 url: config.api + url,
106:                 data: qs.stringify(data),
107:                 timeout: config.timeout,
108:                 headers: {
109:                     'X-Requested-With': 'XMLHttpRequest',
110:                     'Content-Type': 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded; charset=UTF-8',
111:                 },
112:             })
113:             const res = checkStatus(response)
114:             return checkCode(res)
115:         },
116:         async get(url, params) {
117:             const response = await axios({
118:                 method: 'get',
119:                 url: config.api + url,
120:                 params,
121:                 timeout: config.timeout,
122:                 headers: {
123:                     'X-Requested-With': 'XMLHttpRequest',
124:                 },
125:             })
126:             const res = checkStatus(response)
127:             return checkCode(res)
128:         },
129:     }
130: }
131: 
132: export default api()

(End of file - total 132 lines)
</content>
```

65: }

129:         ],
130:     },
131: 
132:     { name: '404', path: '/:catchAll(.*)', component: NotFound },
133: ]
134: 
135: export function createRouter(store: Pinia) {
136:     const router = _createRouter({
137:         // 为服务器/客户端使用适当的历史实现 import.meta.env.SSR 由 Vite 注入。
138:         history: import.meta.env.SSR ? createMemoryHistory() : createWebHistory(),
139:         routes,
140:     })
141: 
142:     const slideLeft = 'slide-left'
143:     const slideRight = 'slide-right'
144: 
145:     router.beforeEach((to, from, next) => {
146:         const appShellStore = useAppShellStore(store)
147:         const { needPageTransition } = storeToRefs(appShellStore)
148:         // 如果不需要切换动画，直接返回
149:         if (needPageTransition.value) {
150:             // 根据 alwaysBackPage, alwaysForwardPage 来判断切换动画
151:             // 判断当前是前进还是后退，添加不同的动画效果
152:             // const pageTransitionName = isForward(to, from) ? slideLeft : slideRight
153:             // =================== //
154:             // 根据路由中的 meta.index 来判断切换动画
155:             let pageTransitionName: string
156:             if (!from.meta.index || to.meta.index === from.meta.index) {
157:                 pageTransitionName = 'fade'
158:             }
159:             else if ((to.meta.index as number) > (from.meta.index as number)) {
160:                 pageTransitionName = slideLeft
161:             }
162:             else {
163:                 pageTransitionName = slideRight
164:             }
165: 
166:             appShellStore.setPageTransitionName(pageTransitionName)
167:         }
168:         next()
169:     })
170: 
171:     router.beforeResolve(async (to, from) => {
172:         let diffed = false
173:         const activated = to.matched.filter((c, i) => {
174:             return diffed || (diffed = from.matched[i] !== c) || from.path !== to.path
175:         })
176: 
177:         if (!activated.length) {
178:             return false
179:         }
180: 
181:         await Promise.all(
182:             activated.map((c) => {
183:                 if ((c.components?.default as any).asyncData) {
184:                     return (c.components?.default as any).asyncData({ store, route: to })
185:                 }
186: 
187:                 return true
188:             }),
189:         )
190:     })
191: 
192:     return router
193: }

(End of file - total 193 lines)

It is a zero-player game, meaning that its evolution is determined by its initial state, requiring no further input. One interacts with the Game of Life by creating an initial configuration and observing how it evolves. It is Turing complete and can simulate a universal constructor or any other Turing machine.

100: 
101: interface Data {
102:     controlsHidden: boolean
103:     inputEnabled: boolean
104:     playEnabled: boolean
105:     intervalId: number
106:     generation: number
107:     grid: Array<Array<boolean>>
108: }
109: 
110: const CellState = {
111:     DEAD: false,
112:     ALIVE: true,
113: }
114: 
115: const controlsHidden = ref(false)
116: const inputEnabled = ref(true)
117: const playEnabled = ref(false)
118: const generation = ref(0)
119: const intervalId = ref(0)
120: const grid = ref<Array<Array<boolean>>>([])
121: 
122: // 初始化网格
123: const initGrid = () => {
124:     cellsX = Math.floor(innerWidth / 16)
125:     cellsY = Math.floor(innerHeight / 16)
126:     
127:     const newGrid: Array<Array<boolean>> = []
128:     for (let i = 0; i < cellsY; i++) {
129:         const row = new Array(cellsX).fill(CellState.DEAD)
130:         for (let j = 0; j < cellsX; j++) {
131:             if (Math.random() < 0.2) {
132:                 row[j] = !CellState.DEAD
133:             }
134:         }
135:         newGrid.push(row)
136:     }
137:     grid.value = newGrid
138: }
139: 
140: const nullCheck = (y: number | null, x: number | null): boolean | null => {
141:     return y !== null && x !== null ? grid.value[y][x].valueOf() : null
142: }
143: 
144: const neighbours = (outerKey: number, innerKey: number): number => {
145:     const leftX = innerKey - 1 < 0 ? null : innerKey - 1
146:     const rightX = innerKey + 1 >= grid.value[outerKey].length ? null : innerKey + 1
147:     const centerX = innerKey
148:     const centerY = outerKey
149:     const topY = outerKey - 1 < 0 ? null : outerKey - 1
150:     const bottomY = outerKey + 1 >= grid.value.length ? null : outerKey + 1
151: 
152:     return [
153:         nullCheck(topY, leftX),
154:         nullCheck(topY, centerX),
155:         nullCheck(topY, rightX),
156:         nullCheck(centerY, leftX),
157:         nullCheck(centerY, rightX),
158:         nullCheck(bottomY, leftX),
159:         nullCheck(bottomY, centerX),
160:         nullCheck(bottomY, rightX),
161:     ].filter(x => x).length
162: }
163: 
164: const userInput = (ok: number, ik: number): void => {
165:     if (inputEnabled.value) {
166:         grid.value = grid.value.map((row, a_ok) => {
167:             return a_ok === ok ? row.map((cell, a_ik) => {
168:                 return a_ik === ik ? !cell : cell
169:             }) : row
170:         })
171:     }
172: }
173: 
174: const step = (): void => {
175:     generation.value++
176:     grid.value = grid.value.map((row, ok) => {
177:         return row.map((cell, ik) => {
178:             if (neighbours(ok, ik) === 3) {
179:                 return CellState.ALIVE
180:             }
181:             if (neighbours(ok, ik) <= 1) {
182:                 return CellState.DEAD
183:             }
184:             if (neighbours(ok, ik) >= 4) {
185:                 return CellState.DEAD
186:             }
187:             return cell
188:         })
189:     })
190: }
191: 
192: const togglePlay = (): void => {
193:     if (playEnabled.value) {
194:         clearInterval(intervalId.value)
195:     }
196:     else {
197:         intervalId.value = setInterval(step, SPEED)
198:     }
199:     playEnabled.value = !playEnabled.value
200: }
201: 
202: const toggleIcon = (): void => {
203:     controlsHidden.value = window.pageYOffset > 150
204: }
205: 
206: onMounted(() => {
207:     initGrid()
208:     window.addEventListener('scroll', toggleIcon)
209: })
210: 
211: onUnmounted(() => {
212:     window.removeEventListener('scroll', toggleIcon)
213:     if (intervalId.value) {
214:         clearInterval(intervalId.value)
215:     }
216: })
217:

<content>1: export function useReceiveStreamData(handleProcessMessage: Function,
2:     beforeSend?: Function) {
3:     async function handleStreamResponse(response: Response) {
4:         const reader = response.body?.getReader()
5:         const decoder = new TextDecoder('utf-8')
6:         // 初始消息
7:         beforeSend && beforeSend()
8:         async function read() {
9:             if (!reader) {
10:                 console.error('Reader is not available.')
11:                 return
12:             }
13:             const result: ReadableStreamReadResult<Uint8Array> = await reader.read()
14:             const { done, value } = result
15:             if (done) {
16:                 console.log('Connection closed')
17:                 return
18:             }
19:             const messageData = decoder.decode(value, { stream: true })
20:             const messages = messageData.split('\n')
21:             for (const msg of messages) {
22:                 if (!processMessage(msg)) {
23:                     return // 如果返回 false，则结束处理
24:                 }
25:             }
26:             await read() // 继续读取后续的数据
27:         }
28:         if (reader) {
29:             await read()
30:         }
31:     }
32: 
33:     function processMessage(msg: string) {
34:         const jsonString = msg.replace(/^data: /, '').trim()
35:         if (jsonString === '[DONE]') {
36:             console.log('Stream completed')
37:             return false // 表示结束处理
38:         }
39:         if (jsonString) {
40:             try {
41:                 const json = JSON.parse(jsonString)
42:                 handleProcessMessage(json)
43:             }
44:             catch (error) {
45:                 console.error('Failed to parse message:', error)
46:             }
47:         }
48:         return true // 表示继续处理
49:     }
50: 
51:     return { handleStreamResponse }
52: }

(End of file - total 52 lines)
